The price is not expensive. Compared with five stars, I would rather rate it ten stars. I took more than 60 photos and videos, and I really can't put them down. Culture and beauty are everywhere!

Whether it is the garden design, architecture, vegetation, flowers, birds, fish and insects of pavilions and terraces, or even small tea cups, they are all ingenious [strong][strong][strong] The boss is a scholar with a very rich cultural heritage.

According to the introduction, the total area is 1,200 acres, with off-road vehicle venues, fishing gardens, and one of Mr. Hu Shi's former residences. The Qingming Riverside Scene, the Great Wall, root carvings, the meticulous carvings of corridors and pavilions, and the carved screens of the four gentlemen of plum, orchid, bamboo and chrysanthemum... It's so shocking! There are only 64 rooms on the second floor.
The room was clean and tidy, with a sense of Zen. Earplugs (actually no noise at all), fruit, coffee were provided. I didn't have time to eat breakfast, so I was given milk cake. The hardware facilities are very highüëç

posted:Posted April 9, 2024
msg:Let me first talk about what everyone is generally concerned about: the new hotel opened in 2023, the facilities and services are impeccable, I think they are all 5-star. I was picked up and dropped off by a free car, and my flight was at 5:30pm, and I could check out late.

What I want to talk about are other special places. It is a very unique courtyard of Jiangnan Hui-style architecture, with white walls and green tiles, horse head walls, archways, and stages, some of which are even hundreds of years old and have a mottled history. It is in a tourist park, and there is also a former residence of Hu Shi inside.

I stayed there for a day, and it happened to be cloudy, night, and sunny. I took a lot of photos with my iPhone. These buildings themselves are historical relics. There are all kinds of fish, insects, flowers and plants on the wood carvings, dragons, phoenixes, (happy) birds, fish, elephants, unicorns, deer (lu), and fortune (bats). There are various modes, such as nine dragons playing with pearls, nine lions rolling beads, double dragons playing with pearls, dragons and phoenixes, and both fortune (bats) and longevity (peach). Friends who are interested in architecture or traditional culture and photography will linger here.

msg:Newly built old building
The first thing you feel when you step into the courtyard is like an elegant small building accidentally found in the ancient times. It is quiet, simple, stylish and sentimental. Each stone brick and beam has weathered and mottled ancient history. The architecture seems to be telling the moving story of the country, the nation, and Hu Shi‚Äôs family.
In particular, the old archway and the old stage next to the lobby are old Hui-style buildings from a hundred years ago. Skilled craftsmen recycled them from the ancient towns of Anhui. They numbered the bricks and tiles with markers and then moved them here as a whole before assembling them. .
Lizheng Courtyard
